Upgrading from 3.x to 4.x","permalink: /docs/upgrading/3-to-4/","---","","A few things have changed in Jekyll 4.","","Before we dive in, you need to have at least Ruby {{ site.data.ruby.min_version }}","installed.","","Run the following in your terminal to check","","```sh","ruby -v","{{ site.data.ruby.current_version_output }}","```","","If you're using a supported Ruby version \u003e= {{ site.data.ruby.min_version }}, go ahead","and fetch the latest version of Jekyll:","","```sh","gem update jekyll","```","","\u003cdiv class=\"note warning\"\u003e","  \u003ch5\u003e\u003ccode\u003epost_url\u003c/code\u003e Tag and Baseurl\u003c/h5\u003e","  \u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e","  \u003cp\u003e","    The \u003ccode\u003epost_url\u003c/code\u003e tag now incorporates the \u003ccode\u003erelative_url\u003c/code\u003e filter within itself","    and therefore automatically prepends your site's \u003ccode\u003ebaseurl\u003c/code\u003e to the post's \u003ccode\u003eurl\u003c/code\u003e","    value.","  \u003c/p\u003e","  \u003cp\u003e","    Please ensure that you change all instances of the \u003ccode\u003epost_url\u003c/code\u003e usage as following:","  \u003c/p\u003e","","{% highlight diff %}","{% raw %}","- {{ site.baseurl }}/{% post_url 2018-03-20-hello-world.markdown %}","+ {% post_url 2018-03-20-hello-world.markdown %}","{% endraw %}","{% endhighlight %}","\u003c/div\u003e","","## Template rendering","","We've slightly altered the way Jekyll parses and renders your various templates","to improve the overall build times. Jekyll now parses a template once, caches it","internally and then renders the parsed template multiple times as required by","your pages and documents.","","The downside to this is that some of the community-authored plugins may not work","as they previously used to.","","## Static files in unrendered collections","","Collections other than `posts` can contain static assets along with Markdown files.","But if the collection has not been configured with metadata `output: true`, then","neither its *documents* nor its *static assets* will be output to the destination","directory.","","## For plugin authors","","* If your plugin depends on the following code: `site.liquid_renderer.file(path).parse(content)`,","note that the return value (`template`, an instance of *`Liquid::Template`*), from that line will","always be the **same object** for a given `path`. \u003cbr/\u003e","The *`template`* instance is then rendered as previously, with respect to the `payload` passed to it.","You'll therefore have to ensure that *`payload`* is not memoized or cached in your plugin instance.","","* If its a requirement that `template` you get from the above step *be different* at all times,","you can invoke *`Liquid::Template`* directly:","","  ```diff","  - template = site.liquid_renderer.file(path).parse(content)","  + template = Liquid::Template.parse(content)","  ```","","## Exclusion changes","","We've enhanced our default exclusion array.","It now looks like the following:","","```yaml","# default excludes","exclude:","- .sass-cache/","- .jekyll-cache/","- gemfiles/","- Gemfile","- Gemfile.lock","- node_modules/","- vendor/bundle/","- vendor/cache/","- vendor/gems/","- vendor/ruby/","```","","What's new is that this array **does not get overridden by the `exclude` array","in the user's config file anymore**. The user's exclude entries simply get","**added** to the above default array (if the entry isn't already excluded).","","To forcibly \"process\" directories or files that have been excluded, list them","in the `include` array instead:","","```yaml","# overrides your excluded items configuration and the default include array ([\".htaccess\"])","include:","  - .htaccess","  - node_modules/uglifier/index.js","```","","The above configuration directs Jekyll to handle only","`node_modules/uglifier/index.js` while ignoring every other file in the","`node_modules` directory since that directory is \"excluded\" by default.","","Note that the default `include` array still gets overridden by the `include`","array in your config file. So, be sure to add `.htaccess` to the list if you","need that file to be present in the generated site.","","## Kramdown v2","","Jekyll has dropped support for `kramdown-1.x` entirely.","","From [`v2.0` onwards](https://kramdown.gettalong.org/news.html#kramdown-200-released)","kramdown requires specific extensions to be additionally installed to use","certain desired features outside of kramdown's core functionality.","","Out of all the extensions listed in the report linked above, gem","`kramdown-parser-gfm` is automatically installed along with Jekyll 4.0. The","remaining extensions will have to be manually installed by the user depending on","desired functionality, by listing the extension's gem-name in their `Gemfile`.","","Notes:","  * `kramdown-converter-pdf` will be ignored by Jekyll Core. To have Jekyll convert Markdown to PDF","    you'll have to depend on a plugin that subclasses `Jekyll::Converter` with the","    [required methods]({% link _docs/plugins/converters.md %}).","","    For example:","","    ```ruby","    module Jekyll","      External.require_with_graceful_fail \"kramdown-converter-pdf\"","","      class Markdown2PDF \u003c Converter","        safe true","        priority :low","","        def matches(ext)","          # match only files that have an extension exactly \".markdown\"","          ext =~ /^\\.markdown$/","        end","","        def convert(content)","          Kramdown::Document.new(content).to_pdf","        end","","        def output_ext","          \".pdf\"","        end","      end","    end","    ```","","  * Vendors that provide a versioned Jekyll Environment Image (e.g. Docker Image, GitHub Pages, etc)","    will have to manually whitelist kramdown's extension gems in their distributions for Jekyll 4.0.","","## Deprecated Configuration Options","","Jekyll 4.0 has dropped support for all legacy configuration options that were deprecated over multiple","releases in the previous series.","","To that end, we shall no longer output a deprecation warning when we encounter a legacy config key nor","shall we gracefully assign their values to the newer counterparts. Depending on the key, it shall either","be ignored or raise an `InvalidConfigurationError` error if the key is still valid but the associated","value is not of the valid type."],"stylingDirectives":[[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[[0,5,"pl-ent"],[7,32,"pl-s"]],[[0,9,"pl-ent"],[11,34,"pl-s"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,5,"pl-en"]],[],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[],[],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,5,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[1,4,"pl-ent"],[5,10,"pl-e"],[11,12,"pl-s"],[12,24,"pl-s"],[24,25,"pl-s"]],[[3,5,"pl-ent"],[7,11,"pl-ent"],[22,26,"pl-ent"],[45,47,"pl-ent"]],[[3,4,"pl-ent"],[5,11,"pl-c1"],[6,10,"pl-k"],[13,14,"pl-ent"]],[[3,4,"pl-ent"]],[[4,101,"pl-c1"]],[[4,104,"pl-c1"]],[[4,10,"pl-c1"]],[[4,5,"pl-ent"]],[[3,4,"pl-ent"]],[[4,96,"pl-c1"]],[[4,5,"pl-ent"]],[],[],[],[[0,1,"pl-v"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"]],[],[],[[2,5,"pl-ent"]],[],[[0,21,"pl-mh"],[3,21,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[[0,41,"pl-mh"],[3,41,"pl-en"]],[],[[23,24,"pl-s"],[24,29,"pl-c1"],[29,30,"pl-s"]],[[60,61,"pl-s"],[61,73,"pl-c1"],[73,74,"pl-s"]],[[12,13,"pl-s"],[22,23,"pl-s"],[32,33,"pl-s"],[46,47,"pl-s"]],[],[],[[0,21,"pl-mh"],[3,21,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[48,49,"pl-s"],[49,95,"pl-c1"],[95,96,"pl-s"]],[[28,29,"pl-s"],[29,37,"pl-c1"],[37,38,"pl-s"],[55,56,"pl-s"],[56,57,"pl-s"],[57,73,"pl-c1"],[73,74,"pl-s"],[74,75,"pl-s"]],[[14,16,"pl-s"],[27,29,"pl-s"],[42,43,"pl-s"],[43,47,"pl-c1"],[47,48,"pl-s"],[51,53,"pl-ent"]],[[4,5,"pl-s"],[5,6,"pl-s"],[6,14,"pl-c1"],[14,15,"pl-s"],[15,16,"pl-s"],[78,79,"pl-s"],[79,86,"pl-c1"],[86,87,"pl-s"]],[[37,38,"pl-s"],[38,39,"pl-s"],[39,46,"pl-c1"],[46,47,"pl-s"],[47,48,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[28,29,"pl-s"],[29,37,"pl-c1"],[37,38,"pl-s"],[67,68,"pl-s"],[80,81,"pl-s"]],[[15,16,"pl-s"],[16,17,"pl-s"],[17,33,"pl-c1"],[33,34,"pl-s"],[34,35,"pl-s"]],[],[[2,5,"pl-s"],[5,9,"pl-en"]],[],[],[[2,5,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,20,"pl-mh"],[3,20,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-en"]],[[0,18,"pl-c"],[0,1,"pl-c"]],[[0,7,"pl-ent"]],[[2,14,"pl-s"]],[[2,16,"pl-s"]],[[2,11,"pl-s"]],[[2,9,"pl-s"]],[[2,14,"pl-s"]],[[2,15,"pl-s"]],[[2,16,"pl-s"]],[[2,15,"pl-s"]],[[2,14,"pl-s"]],[[2,14,"pl-s"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[0,1,"pl-pds"],[1,2,"pl-pds"],[2,3,"pl-pds" aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
  <tbody>
  <tr>
    <th>title</th>
    <td>Upgrading from 3.x to 4.x</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <th>permalink</th>
    <td>/docs/upgrading/3-to-4/</td>
  </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<p dir="auto">A few things have changed in Jekyll 4.</p>
<p dir="auto">Before we dive in, you need to have at least Ruby {{ site.data.ruby.min_version }}
installed.</p>
<p dir="auto">Run the following in your terminal to check</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="ruby -v
{{ site.data.ruby.current_version_output }}"><pre>ruby -v
{{ site.data.ruby.current_version_output }}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you're using a supported Ruby version &gt;= {{ site.data.ruby.min_version }}, go ahead
and fetch the latest version of Jekyll:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gem update jekyll"><pre>gem update jekyll</pre></div>
<div dir="auto">
  <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>post_url</code> Tag and Baseurl</h5><a id="user-content-post_url-tag-and-baseurl" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: post_url Tag and Baseurl" href="#post_url-tag-and-baseurl"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
  <p dir="auto"> </p>
  <p dir="auto">
    The <code>post_url</code> tag now incorporates the <code>relative_url</code> filter within itself
    and therefore automatically prepends your site's <code>baseurl</code> to the post's <code>url</code>
    value.
  </p>
  <p dir="auto">
    Please ensure that you change all instances of the <code>post_url</code> usage as following:
  </p>
<p dir="auto">{% highlight diff %}
{% raw %}</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>{{ site.baseurl }}/{% post_url 2018-03-20-hello-world.markdown %}</li>
</ul>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>{% post_url 2018-03-20-hello-world.markdown %}
{% endraw %}
{% endhighlight %}</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Template rendering</h2><a id="user-content-template-rendering" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Template rendering" href="#template-rendering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We've slightly altered the way Jekyll parses and renders your various templates
to improve the overall build times. Jekyll now parses a template once, caches it
internally and then renders the parsed template multiple times as required by
your pages and documents.</p>
<p dir="auto">The downside to this is that some of the community-authored plugins may not work
as they previously used to.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Static files in unrendered collections</h2><a id="user-content-static-files-in-unrendered-collections" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Static files in unrendered collections" href="#static-files-in-unrendered-collections"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Collections other than <code>posts</code> can contain static assets along with Markdown files.
But if the collection has not been configured with metadata <code>output: true</code>, then
neither its <em>documents</em> nor its <em>static assets</em> will be output to the destination
directory.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">For plugin authors</h2><a id="user-content-for-plugin-authors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: For plugin authors" href="#for-plugin-authors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">If your plugin depends on the following code: <code>site.liquid_renderer.file(path).parse(content)</code>,
note that the return value (<code>template</code>, an instance of <em><code>Liquid::Template</code></em>), from that line will
always be the <strong>same object</strong> for a given <code>path</code>. <br>
The <em><code>template</code></em> instance is then rendered as previously, with respect to the <code>payload</code> passed to it.
You'll therefore have to ensure that <em><code>payload</code></em> is not memoized or cached in your plugin instance.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If its a requirement that <code>template</code> you get from the above step <em>be different</em> at all times,
you can invoke <em><code>Liquid::Template</code></em> directly:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="- template = site.liquid_renderer.file(path).parse(content)
+ template = Liquid::Template.parse(content)"><pre><span class="pl-md"><span class="pl-md">-</span> template = site.liquid_renderer.file(path).parse(content)</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span> template = Liquid::Template.parse(content)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Exclusion changes</h2><a id="user-content-exclusion-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Exclusion changes" href="#exclusion-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We've enhanced our default exclusion array.
It now looks like the following:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# default excludes
exclude:
- .sass-cache/
- .jekyll-cache/
- gemfiles/
- Gemfile
- Gemfile.lock
- node_modules/
- vendor/bundle/
- vendor/cache/
- vendor/gems/
- vendor/ruby/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> default excludes</span>
<span class="pl-ent">exclude</span>:
- <span class="pl-s">.sass-cache/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">.jekyll-cache/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">gemfiles/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">Gemfile</span>
- <span class="pl-s">Gemfile.lock</span>
- <span class="pl-s">node_modules/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">vendor/bundle/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">vendor/cache/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">vendor/gems/</span>
- <span class="pl-s">vendor/ruby/</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">What's new is that this array <strong>does not get overridden by the <code>exclude</code> array
in the user's config file anymore</strong>. The user's exclude entries simply get
<strong>added</strong> to the above default array (if the entry isn't already excluded).</p>
<p dir="auto">To forcibly "process" directories or files that have been excluded, list them
in the <code>include</code> array instead:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# overrides your excluded items configuration and the default include array ([&quot;.htaccess&quot;])
include:
  - .htaccess
  - node_modules/uglifier/index.js"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> overrides your excluded items configuration and the default include array ([".htaccess"])</span>
<span class="pl-ent">include</span>:
  - <span class="pl-s">.htaccess</span>
  - <span class="pl-s">node_modules/uglifier/index.js</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The above configuration directs Jekyll to handle only
<code>node_modules/uglifier/index.js</code> while ignoring every other file in the
<code>node_modules</code> directory since that directory is "excluded" by default.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that the default <code>include</code> array still gets overridden by the <code>include</code>
array in your config file. So, be sure to add <code>.htaccess</code> to the list if you
need that file to be present in the generated site.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Kramdown v2</h2><a id="user-content-kramdown-v2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Kramdown v2" href="#kramdown-v2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Jekyll has dropped support for <code>kramdown-1.x</code> entirely.</p>
<p dir="auto">From <a href="https://kramdown.gettalong.org/news.html#kramdown-200-released" rel="nofollow"><code>v2.0</code> onwards</a>
kramdown requires specific extensions to be additionally installed to use
certain desired features outside of kramdown's core functionality.</p>
<p dir="auto">Out of all the extensions listed in the report linked above, gem
<code>kramdown-parser-gfm</code> is automatically installed along with Jekyll 4.0. The
remaining extensions will have to be manually installed by the user depending on
desired functionality, by listing the extension's gem-name in their <code>Gemfile</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Notes:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>kramdown-converter-pdf</code> will be ignored by Jekyll Core. To have Jekyll convert Markdown to PDF
you'll have to depend on a plugin that subclasses <code>Jekyll::Converter</code> with the
[required methods]({% link _docs/plugins/converters.md %}).</p>
<p dir="auto">For example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="module Jekyll
  External.require_with_graceful_fail &quot;kramdown-converter-pdf&quot;

  class Markdown2PDF &lt; Converter
    safe true
    priority :low

    def matches(ext)
      # match only files that have an extension exactly &quot;.markdown&quot;
      ext =~ /^\.markdown$/
    end

    def convert(content)
      Kramdown::Document.new(content).to_pdf
    end

    def output_ext
      &quot;.pdf&quot;
    end
  end
end"><pre><span class="pl-k">module</span> <span class="pl-v">Jekyll</span>
  <span class="pl-v">External</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">require_with_graceful_fail</span> <span class="pl-s">"kramdown-converter-pdf"</span>

  <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Markdown2PDF</span> &lt; <span class="pl-v">Converter</span>
    <span class="pl-en">safe</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    <span class="pl-en">priority</span> <span class="pl-pds">:low</span>

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">matches</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">ext</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
      <span class="pl-c"># match only files that have an extension exactly ".markdown"</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">ext</span> =~ <span class="pl-sr">/^<span class="pl-cce">\.</span>markdown$/</span>
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">convert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">content</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
      <span class="pl-v">Kramdown</span>::<span class="pl-v">Document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">new</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">content</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to_pdf</span>
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">output_ext</span>
      <span class="pl-s">".pdf"</span>
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
  <span class="pl-k">end</span>
<span class="pl-k">end</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Vendors that provide a versioned Jekyll Environment Image (e.g. Docker Image, GitHub Pages, etc)
will have to manually whitelist kramdown's extension gems in their distributions for Jekyll 4.0.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Deprecated Configuration Options</h2><a id="user-content-deprecated-configuration-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Deprecated Configuration Options" href="#deprecated-configuration-options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Jekyll 4.0 has dropped support for all legacy configuration options that were deprecated over multiple
releases in the previous series.</p>
<p dir="auto">To that end, we shall no longer output a deprecation warning when we encounter a legacy config key nor
shall we gracefully assign their values to the newer counterparts. Depending on the key, it shall either
be ignored or raise an <code>InvalidConfigurationError</code> error if the key is still valid but the associated
value is not of the valid type.</p>
</article></div><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><button hidden="" data-testid="" data-hotkey-scope="read-only-cursor-text-area"></button><button hidden=""></button></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
